<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Scripts để auto-save variables</h3><a id="user-content-scripts-để-auto-save-variables" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Scripts để auto-save variables" href="#scripts-để-auto-save-variables"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Thêm vào Tests tab của mỗi request:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// Sau khi login/register
if (pm.response.code === 200 || pm.response.code === 201) {
    const response = pm.response.json();
    
    // Lấy user data từ response
    const userData = response.data || response;
    const userId = userData._id || response._id;
    const userRole = userData.role || response.role;
    
    // Lưu token và user ID theo role
    if (response.token) {
        if (userRole === 'admin') {
            pm.environment.set(&quot;admin_token&quot;, response.token);
            pm.environment.set(&quot;admin_id&quot;, userId);
        } else {
            pm.environment.set(&quot;token&quot;, response.token);
            pm.environment.set(&quot;user_id&quot;, userId);
        }
    }
}

// Sau khi create category
if (pm.response.code === 201) {
    const response = pm.response.json();
    if (response.data &amp;&amp; response.data._id) {
        pm.environment.set(&quot;category_id&quot;, response.data._id);
    } else if (response._id) {
        pm.environment.set(&quot;category_id&quot;, response._id);
    }
}

// Sau khi create book
if (pm.response.code === 201) {
    const response = pm.response.json();
    if (response.data &amp;&amp; response.data._id) {
        // Lưu book đầu tiên
        if (!pm.environment.get(&quot;book_id&quot;)) {
            pm.environment.set(&quot;book_id&quot;, response.data._id);
        } else {
            // Lưu book thứ hai
            pm.environment.set(&quot;book_id_2&quot;, response.data._id);
        }
    }
}

// Sau khi create coupon
if (pm.response.code === 201) {
    const response = pm.response.json();
    if (response.data &amp;&amp; response.data._id) {
        pm.environment.set(&quot;coupon_id&quot;, response.data._id);
    }
}

// Sau khi create review
if (pm.response.code === 201) {
    const response = pm.response.json();
    if (response.data &amp;&amp; response.data._id) {
        pm.environment.set(&quot;review_id&quot;, response.data._id);
    }
}

// Sau khi create order
if (pm.response.code === 201) {
    const response = pm.response.json();
    if (response.data &amp;&amp; response.data._id) {
        pm.environment.set(&quot;order_id&quot;, response.data._id);
    }

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Notes</h2><a id="user-content-notes" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Notes" href="#notes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>Thứ tự quan trọng</strong>: Phải test theo đúng thứ tự từ Level 1 → Level 5</li>
<li><strong>Data Dependencies</strong>: Mỗi level phụ thuộc vào data từ level trước</li>
<li><strong>Admin Account</strong>: Cần tạo admin account trước để test admin features</li>
<li><strong>Environment Cleanup</strong>: Sau mỗi test cycle, có thể cần reset database</li>
<li><strong>Token Expiration</strong>: Token có thể hết hạn, cần login lại nếu gặp 401 errors</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Expected Results Summary</h2><a id="user-content-expected-results-summary" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Expected Results Summary" href="#expected-results-summary"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<li><strong>Level 1</strong>: Base modules hoạt động độc lập ✓</li>
